            <div n="1" type="sthāna">

                <head xml:lang="en">[Sūtrasthāna 32-end]</head>

                <div n="32" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 32, draft based on MS H]</head>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.1"><label>1.32.1</label> athātaḥ
                        svabhāvavipratipattiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.3-4"><label>1.32.3-4</label> svabhāvaprasiddhānāṃ
                        śarīraikadeśānām anyathātvaṃ maraṇāya | tad yathā śuklānāṃ
                        kṛṣṇatvaṃ kṛṣṇānāṃ śuklatvaṃ | sthirāṇām mṛdutvaṃ | calānām
                        acalatvam acalānāñ calatvaṃ | pṛthūnāṃ saṃkṣiptatvaṃ saṃkṣiptānāṃ
                        pṛthutvaṃ | dīrghāṇāṃ hrasvatvaṃ ca hrasvānāṃ dīrghatā |
                        apatanadharmmiṇāṃ patanam akasmāc
                        chaityoṣṇasneharaukṣyaprastambhavaivarṇṇyāni apasarppaṇam aṅgānāṃ
                        svebhyaḥ sthānebhyaḥ śarīraikadeśānām
                        avasraṃsotkṣiptabhrāntapatitavimuktanirggamātigamagurulaghutvāni
                        pravālavarṇṇavyaṅgaprādurbbhāvo vākasmāt sirāṇāṃ ca darśana lalāṭe
                        nāsāvaṃśe vā piṭakotpattir udakotpattir nnetrarogam
                        vināsrupravṛttir lalāṭe vā prabhātakāle svedapravṛttiḥ |
                        gomayacūrṇṇaprakāśasya rajaso darśanam uttamāṅge līyanam vā
                        kapotakaṅkagṛddhraprabhṛtīnāṃ mūtrapurīṣapravṛddhir abhuñjanānāṃ
                        stanamūlahṛdayorassu ca śūlotpattayaḥ | madhye śūnatvam anteṣu
                        parimlāyitvaṃ | viparyayo vā naṣṭahīnavikalavihṛtasvaraṃ vā
                        vivarṇṇapuṣpaprādurbbhāvo vā dantanakhaśarīreṣu puṣpadarśanaṃ
                        yasya cāpsu kaphaśakṛdretāṃsi nimajjanti yasya ca dṛṣṭimaṇḍale
                        bhinnavikṛtāni rūpāṇy ālocyante snehābhyaktakeśāṅga iva yo bhāti
                        yaś ca durbbalo bhaktadveṣātisārābhyām pīḍyate | kāsamānaś ca
                        tṛṣṇātibhūtaḥ kṣīṇaś charddibhaktadeśayuktaḥ saphenarudhirodvāmī
                        hatasvaraḥ śūlābhihataś ca manuṣyaśūnakaracaraṇo nnadveṣī
                        srastapiṇḍakāṃsapāṇipādaḥ | yaś ca pūrvāhṇe bhuktam aparāhṇe
                        ścharddayaty avidagdhaṃ sāryate vā jvarakāsābhibhūtaḥ sa śvāsān
                        mriyate | vastavad vilapamāno bhūmau patati srastamuṣkaḥ
                        stabdhaśepo bhagnagrīvaḥ praṇaṣṭamehaś ca manuṣyaḥ
                        prāgviśuṣyamāṇahṛdaya ārddraśarīraḥ | yaś ca loṣṭaṃ
                        loṣṭenābhihanti | kāṣṭham vā kāṣṭhena tṛṇāni vā cchinnanti |
                        adharoṣṭham vā daśati uttaroṣṭham vā leḍhi | āluñcati karṇṇau
                        keśām̐ś ca | devadvijagurusuhṛdvaidyān vā vidveṣṭi yasya ca
                        vakrānuvakragā grahā garhitasthānagatāḥ | janmaṛkṣam
                        vāsyolkāśanibhyām abhihanyate | rātrau vā
                        gṛhadvāraśayanāśanayānavāhanamaṇiratnopakaraṇagarhitalakṣaṇanimittaprādurbbhāvo
                        veti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.5"><label>1.32.5</label> bhavanti cātra || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.5ab"><label>1.32.5ab</label> cikitsyamānaḥ samyak
                        tu vikāro yo bhivarddhate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.5cd"><label>1.32.5cd</label> prakṣīṇabalamāṃsasya
                        lakṣaṇan tadgatāyuṣaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.6ab"><label>1.32.6ab</label> nivarttate mahāvyādhiḥ
                        sahasā yasya dehinaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.6cd"><label>1.32.6cd</label> na cāhāraphalaṃ yasya
                        dṛśyate sa vinaśyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.7ab"><label>1.32.7ab</label> etāni riṣṭarūpāṇi
                        samyag budhyeta yo bhiṣak | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.32.7cd"><label>1.32.7cd</label> sādhyāsādhyaparīkṣañ
                        ca sa rājñaḥ sammato bhaved iti || 31 || ❈ || </l>

                </div>

                <div n="33" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 33, draft based on MS H]</head>




                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.1"><label>1.33.1</label> athāto vāraṇīyam adhyāyaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.2"><label>1.33.2</label> upadravais tu ye
                        juṣṭā-vyādhayo yānty avāryatāṃ | rasāyanair vvinā vatsa tāṃ śṛṇv
                        ekamanā <cb n="2"/>mama || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.4"><label>1.33.4</label> vātavyādhiḥ pramehaś ca
                        kuṣṭhānyatha bhagandaraṃ | arśośmarī mūḍhagarbho bhavaty udaram
                        aṣṭamam || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.5"><label>1.33.5</label> aṣṭāv ete mahāntaḥ syūr
                        vvyādhayo dustarāḥ sadā | prāṇamāṃsakṣayaḥ śophas tṛṣṇā ccharddir
                        jvaras tathā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.6"><label>1.33.6</label> atīsāraś ca mūrcchā ca
                        <caesura/>
                         hikkāśvāsas tathaiva ca | etair upadravair jjuṣṭān sarvvān etān
                        vivarjayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.7"><label>1.33.7</label> śūnaṃ suptatvacam bhagnaṅ
                            ka<cb n="2"/>mpādhmānanipīḍitaṃ | rujārttam antañ ca naram
                        vātavyādhir vvināśayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.8"><label>1.33.8</label> yathoktopadravāviṣṭam
                        atiprasrutam eva ca | piṭakāpīḍitaṃ gāḍhaṃ prameho hanti mānavaṃ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.9"><label>1.33.9</label> prabhinnaṃ prasrutāṅgañ ca
                        raktanetraṃ hatasvaraṃ | pañcakarmmaguṇātītaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ hanti hi
                        kuṣṭhinaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.11"><label>1.33.11</label> vātamūtrapurīṣāṇi
                        krimayaḥ śukram eva ca | bhagandarāt prasravanti sa naśyati
                        bhagandarī || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.10"><label>1.33.10</label> tṛṣṇarocakaśūlārttam
                        atiprasrutaśoṇitaṃ | śophātīsārasaṃyuktaṃ durnāmā kṣapayen naraṃ
                        ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.12"><label>1.33.12</label> praśūnanābhivṛṣaṇaṃ
                        vaddhamūtrarujāturaṃ | aśmarī kṣapayaty āśu sikatāśarkkarānvitaṃ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.14"><label>1.33.14</label> pārśvabhaṅgānnavidveṣaḥ
                        śophātīsārapīḍitam | vivarjayed udariṇam virikto yo 'bhipūryate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.13"><label>1.33.13</label> yonīsamvaraṇaṃ saṅgaḥ
                        kukṣo makkallasaṃjñitaḥ | hanyuḥ striyaṃ mūḍhaga-rvbhe yathoktāś
                        cāpy upadravāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.15"><label>1.33.15</label> visaṃjñas tām yate yas
                        tu śete nipati-<cb n="2"/>to yathā | śītārddito 'ntaruṣṇaś ca
                        <caesura/>
                         jvareṇa mriyate naraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.16"><label>1.33.16</label> yo hṛṣṭaromā raktākṣo
                        hṛdi saṃghātaśūlavān | vaktreṇa cocchvasiti taṃ jvaro hanti
                        mānavaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.17"><label>1.33.17</label> hikkāśvāsa samāyuktaṃ
                        mūḍham vibhrāntalocanaṃ | santatocchvāsinaṃ kṣīṇaṃ naraṃ kṣapayate
                        jvaraḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.18"><label>1.33.18</label>
                    </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.19"><label>1.33.19</label>
                        śvāsaśūlapipāsārtaṃ-kṣīṇañ jvaranipīḍitaṃ | viśeṣeṇa naraṃ vṛddham
                        atīsāro vināśayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.20"><label>1.33.20</label> śuklākṣamannadveṣṭāram
                        ūrddhaśvāsanipīḍitam | kṛcchreṇa vahu mehantaṃ yakṣmā hantīha
                        mānavaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.21"><label>1.33.21</label>
                        śvāsaśūlapipāsānnavidveṣo granthimūḍhatā | jāyate durvvalatvaṃ ca
                        gulmino maraṇāya vai|| </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.22"><label>1.33.22</label> ādhmānaṃ vaddhaniṣyandaṃ
                        ccharddihikkātṛṣānvitam | rujāśvāsasamāyuktaṃ vidradhir nnāśayet
                        naraṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.23"><label>1.33.23</label> pāṇḍudantanakho yastu
                        pāṇḍunetraś ca mānavaḥ | pāṇḍusaṃghātadarśī ca pāṇḍurogī vinaśyati
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.24"><label>1.33.24</label> lohitañ charddayed yas
                        tu vahuśo lohitekṣaṇaḥ | lohito ṅgāradarśī ca mriyate
                        raktapaittikaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.25"><label>1.33.25</label> avāco pi savāco 'pi
                        kṣīṇamānsavalo naraḥ | jāgarūko kṣyāsandeham unmādena vinaśyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.33.26"><label>1.33.26</label> apasmarantam vahuśaḥ
                        prakṣīṇañ calitaṃ bhruvaṃ | netrābhyāñ ca vikurvvāṇa-m apasmāro
                        vināśayet ||</l>
                    <p ana="trailer"> 33 ||</p>
                </div>

                <div n="34" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 34, draft based on MS H]</head>




                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.1"><label>1.34.1</label>athāto yuktasenīyaṃ
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.1.1"><label>1.34.1.1</label>dhanvantarim
                        mahāprājñaṃ sarvvaśāstraviśāradaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         caraṇāv upasaṃgṛhya suśrutaḥ paripṛcchati ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.3"><label>1.34.3</label>yuktasenasya nṛpateḥ
                        parānabhijighāṃsataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhiṣajā rakṣaṇaṃ kāryaṃ yathā tad brūhi me mune ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.3.1"><label>1.34.3.1</label>tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā
                        prābravīd bhiṣajām varaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.4"><label>1.34.4</label>vijigīṣuḥ sahāmātyair
                        yātrāyuktaḥ prayatnataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rakṣitavyo viśeṣeṇa viṣādeva narādhipaḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.5"><label>1.34.5</label>panthānam udakañ chāyāṃ
                        bhaktaṃ yavasamindhanaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         duṣayanty arayas tāni jānīyāc chodhanīya ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasya liṅgaṃ cikitsāñ ca kalpasthāne pravakṣyate ||</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.6"><label>1.34.6</label>ekottaraṃ mṛtyuśatam
                        atharvvāṇaḥ pracakṣate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tatraikaḥ kālasaṃyuktaḥ śeṣās tv āgantavaḥ smṛtāḥ |</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.7"><label>1.34.7</label>doṣāgantunimittebhyo
                        rasamantraviśāradau |
                        <caesura/>
                         rakṣatāṃ nṛpatin nityaṃ yatnād vaidyapurohitau ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.8"><label>1.34.8</label>brahmāvedāṅgamaṣṭāṅgam
                        āyurvvedam pracakṣate |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt purohitamate vartteta bhiṣag ātmavān ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.9"><label>1.34.9</label>saṅkaraḥ sarvvavarṇṇānāṃ
                        vināśo dharmmakarmmiṇāṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         prajanām api kṛcchrāṇi bhavanti nṛpanāśataḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.10"><label>1.34.10</label>puruṣāṇān nṛpānāñ ca
                        kevalan tulyamūrttitā |
                        <caesura/>
                         ājñātyāgaḥ kṣamā dhairyam vikramaś cāpy amānuṣaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.11"><label>1.34.11</label>tasmād devam ivābhīkṣṇam
                        vāṅmanaḥ karmabhiḥ śubhaiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         cintayet nṛpatim vaidyaḥ śreyāṃsīcchan vicakṣaṇaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.12"><label>1.34.12</label>skandhāvāre ca mahati
                        rājaveśma samīpataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         bhavet sannihito vaidyaḥ sarvvopakaraṇānvitaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.13"><label>1.34.13</label>tatrastham enan dhvajavad
                        yaśaḥkhyātibhir ucchritaṃ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         upasarppantyamohena viṣaśalyāmayārdditāḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.14"><label>1.34.14</label>svatantrakuśalo 'nyeṣu
                        śāstrārtheṣv abahiḥ kṛtaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaidyo dhvajam ivābhāti nṛpatadvidyapūjitaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.15"><label>1.34.15</label>vaidyo vyādhyupasṛṣṭaś ca
                        bhaiṣajam paricārakaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ete pādāś cikitsāyāḥ karmmasādhanahetavaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.16"><label>1.34.16</label>guṇavadbhis tribhiḥ
                        pādaiś caturthyo guṇavān bhiṣak |
                        <caesura/>
                         vyādhim alpena kālena mahāntam api sādhayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.17"><label>1.34.17</label>vaidyahīnās trayaḥ pādā
                        guṇavanto 'pyapārthakāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         udgātṛhotṛbrahmāṇo yathādhvaryam vinādhvare ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.18"><label>1.34.18</label>vaidyas tu guṇavāneko
                        yāpayed āturaṃ sadā |
                        <caesura/>
                         plavam paricaran dhīraḥ karṇṇadhāram ivāmbhasi ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.19"><label>1.34.19</label>tatvopagataśāstrārtho
                        dṛṣṭakarmmā svayaṅkṛtī |
                        <caesura/>
                         laghuhastaḥ śuciḥ sūraḥ sajjopaskarabheṣajaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.20"><label>1.34.20</label>pratyutpannamatir ddhīmān
                        vyavasāyī viśāradaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         satyadharmmaparo yaś ca sabhiṣak pāda ucyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.21"><label>1.34.21</label>āyuṣmān satvavān sādhyo
                        dravyavān mitravān api |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaidyavākyakṛd āstiṣko vyādhitaḥ pāda ucyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.22"><label>1.34.22</label>praśastadeśasaṃbhūtaṃ
                        praśaste kāla uddhṛtaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yuktamātram manaskāntaṅ gandhavarṇṇarasānvitaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.23"><label>1.34.23</label>doṣaghnamaglāninikaram
                        avikārya viparyayaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         samīkṣya dattaṅ kāle ca bheṣajam pāda ucyate ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.34.24"><label>1.34.24</label>snigdho 'jugupsur
                        bbalavānyukto vyādhitarakṣaṇe |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaidyavākyakṛdaśrāntaḥ pādaḥ paricaraḥ smṛtaḥ ||</l>

                    <p ana="trailer">layka ||</p>
                </div>

                <div n="35" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 35, draft based on MS H]</head>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.1"><label>1.35.1</label> athāta āturopakramanīyam
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.2"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.3"><label>1.35.3</label> āturam upakramamāṇena
                        vaidyenāyurādāveva tāvat parīsatyāyuṣi
                        vyādhyṛtvagnivayodehasatvavalasātmyaprakṛtibheṣajadeśān parīkṣeta
                        | </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.4"><label>1.35.4</label>tatra
                        mahāpāṇipādapṛṣṭhastanāgrasukhadarśanaskandhalalāṭadīrghāṅguliparvvocchvāsaprekṣaṇavāhum
                        vistīrṇṇabhrūs tanāntaroraskaṃ hṛsvajaṅghāmeḍhragrīvaṅ
                        gambhīrasatvasva ranāsim anuccair vaddhastanm upacitamahāromaṃ
                        romasakarṇṇe pārśva mastakaṃ snātānuliptaṃ mūrddham ānūpūrvyo
                        paścāc ca viśuṣyamāṇahṛdayam puruṣañ jānīyād dīrghāyuḥ khalv ayam
                        iti | tam ekāntena upakramet | tatra taillaikṣaṇair viparītair
                        alpayum miśrair mmadhyam āyur iti || bha || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.5"><label>1.35.5</label> gūḍhasandhisirāsnāyuḥ
                        saṃhatāṅgaḥ sthirendriyaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         uttarottarasukṣetro yaḥ sa dīrghāyur ucyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.6"><label>1.35.6</label> garbhāt prabhṛtyarogo yaḥ
                        śanaiḥ samabhivarddhate |
                        <caesura/>
                         śarīrajñānavijñānaiḥ sadīrghāyuḥ samāsataḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.7"><label>1.35.7</label> madhyamasyāyuṣo jñāna mata
                        ūrdhvan nibodha me |
                        <caesura/>
                         adhastād akṣayor yasya rekhāḥ suvyaktam āyatāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.8"><label>1.35.8</label> dve vā tisro 'dhikā vāpi
                        pādau karṇau ca māṃsalau |
                        <caesura/>
                         nāsāgram ūrdhvañ ca bhavet rekhāś ca pṛṣṭhataḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.9"><label>1.35.9</label> yasya syus tasya vijñeyam
                        āyur bhavati saptatiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         jaghanyaś cāyuṣo jñāna mata ūrdhvan nibodha me || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.10"><label>1.35.10</label> hṛsvāni yasya parvvāṇi
                        sumahac cāpi mehanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         avalīḍhamuroyaś ca na ca syāt pṛṣṭham āyataṃ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.11"><label>1.35.11</label> ūrdhvañ ca śravaṇau
                        sthānān nāsā coccā śarīriṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         hasato jalpato vāpi dantamānsam pradṛśyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.12"><label>1.35.12</label> atha punar āyuṣo
                        vijñānārtham aṅgapratyaṅgapramāṇasāra anupadekṣyāmaḥ || tatra
                        aṅgātyantarādhiśakthivāhuśirāṃsi tad avayavāḥ pratyaṅgāni svair
                        aṅgulaiḥ pādāṅguṣṭhapradeśinyau dvaṅgulāyate | pradeśinyās tu
                        madhyamānāmikākaniṣṭhikā pūrvvataḥ | pañcañ
                        bhāgahīnācaturaṅgulāyate | pañcaṅgulavismṛte | </l>



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.13"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.14"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.15"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.16"><label>1.35.16</label>
                        snigdhatāmranakhanayanajihoṣṭhapāṇipādatalaṃ | raktnena suprasanna
                        mṛdutvagromāṇaṃ tvaṣāṃ pūrvva prādhānyād āyuḥ saubhāgyāpayogāyeti
                        ||</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.17"><label>1.35.17</label> sāmānyato
                        'ṅgapratyaṅgapramāṇād atha sārataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         parīkṣyāyuḥ sunipuṇo bhiṣak sidhyati karmmasu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.18"><label>1.35.18</label> vyādhiviśeṣās tu prāg
                        abhihitāḥ sarvvaṃ evaite trividhā bhavanti | sādhyā yāpyāḥ
                        pratyākhyeyāś ceti | tatra sādhya yāpya pratyākhye yān vyādhīn
                        bhūyatri vidhā parīkṣeta | kimayam aupasargikaḥ prāk kevalo
                        'nyalakṣaṇa iti | taraupasargiko nāma yaḥ pūrvvotpannaṃ vyādhiñ
                        jaghanyakālajāto vyādhir upasṛjati | sa tat mūle sa
                        evopadravasaṃjñaḥ | prāk kevalo nāma | yaḥ prāgevotpanno vyādhirar
                        apūrvarūpopadravaś ca | anya lakṣaṇo nāma yo bhaviṣyat khyāpakaḥ
                        sa pūrvvarūpasaṃjñaḥ | tatra sopadravam anyonyāvirodhenopacaret |
                        valavantaram upadravam vā prāk kevalaṃ yathāsvam pratikurvīta |
                        anye lakṣaṇe tv ādivyādhau yathā yathāvat prayateta | b|havati || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.19"><label>1.35.19</label> nāsti rogo vinā doṣaṃ
                        yasmāt tasmāc cikitsakaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         anuktam api doṣāṇāṃ liṅgair doṣamupācaret || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.20"><label>1.35.20</label> prāg abhihitā ṛtavaḥ | </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.21"><label>1.35.21</label> śīta śītapratīkāram uṣṇe

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.22"><label>1.35.22</label> apāpte vā kriyākāle
                        prāpte vā na kṛtā kriyā |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.23"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.24"><label>1.35.24</label> prāg abhihito 'gnir
                        annābhipācakaḥ sa pañcavidho bhavati || samo doṣābhipanno vikriyām
                        āpanna iti || viṣamo vātena | tīkṣṇa pittena | mandaḥ śleṣmaṇā |
                        samaḥ sarvvaiḥ samar iti || tatra yo yathā kālam annam upayuktaṃ
                        samya pacati sa samaḥ | yas tu kadācit samyak pacati kadācid
                        asamyak pacaty ādhmānaśūlātīsārapravāhaṇāni kṛtvā pacati sa
                        viṣamaḥ | yas tu prabhūtampyannam upayuktam āśu pacati sa tīkṣṇaḥ
                        | sarvābhivardhamāno 'tyagnir bhavati || muhumr mmuhuḥ
                        prabhūtataram annam upayuktam āśutaraṃ pacati pākānte ca
                        galatālvoṣṭha praśoṣadāhasantāpān janayati asyaiva bhasmaka iti
                        vyapadiśanti || yas tv alpam apy annam upayuktam
                        udaraśirogauravakāsaśvāsac chardiprasekagātrasadanāni kṛtvā mahā
                        kālena pacati sa mandaḥ || bha || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.25"><label>1.35.25</label> viṣamo vātajān rogāñ
                        stīkṣṇaḥ pittanimittajān |
                        <caesura/>
                         karoty agnis tathā mando vikārān kaphasambhavān || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.26"><label>1.35.26</label> tatra same rakṣaṇaṃ
                        kurvvīta || viṣamaṃ lavaṇāmlaiḥ snehayuktaiḥ kriyāviśeṣair
                        upacaret || tīkṣṇam madhurasnigdhayuktair vvirecanaiś ca | evam
                        evāty agnim viśeṣeṇa māhiyaird dadhikṣīrasarppibhir iti || mande
                        kaṭutiktakaṣāyair vvamanaiś ca || bha || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.27"><label>1.35.27</label> audāryo bhagavān agniḥ

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.28"><label>1.35.28</label> prāṇāpānasamānais tu
                        sarvvataḥ pavanais tribhiḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dhyāmate pālyate cāpi svāṃ svāṃ gatim avasthitaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.29"><label>1.35.29</label> vayas tu trividham
                        vālyaṃ madhyam vṛddham iti | tatronaṣoḍaśavarṣād vālābhavanti | te
                        trividhāḥ kṣīrapāḥ kṣīrānnādā annādā iti | ṣoḍaśasaptatyor antare
                        madhyasvayas tasyad vikalpo vṛddhir yauvanaṃ sampūrṇṇateti |
                        tatrāviṃśater vṛddhir ātriṃśato yauvanam ācatvāriṃśataḥ
                        sarvvadhātvindriyasampūrṇṇetiti || ata ūrdhvaṃ hā nir bhavati
                        yāvadā saptateḥ | saptatyāsrūrdhaṃ
                        kṣīyamāṇadhātvindriyavalavīryotsāho 'nyahani valīpalitakhālity
                        akāsaśvāsaprabhṛtibhir upadravair abhibhūyamānaṃ
                        sarvvakriyāsvasamarthā jīrṇṇāgāram ivāvasīdati | tam vṛddham
                        ācakṣate | </l>

                        'vastjāsu uttarottare bheṣajamātraprayogaḥ | ṛte parihānim
                        kurvanti || bha || </l>

                        sukhatāṃ yāti sevitaḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.41"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.42"><label>1.35.42</label> deśastvānūpo jāṅgalaḥ
                        sādhāraṇa iti trividhā bhavati | tatra
                        nimnonnatavahūdakanadīvarṣagahanamṛdūśītalo vahūmahāparvatavṛkṣo
                        mṛdusukumāropacitaśarīramanuṣyaprāyo vātakapharogabhūyiṣṭhaś
                        cānūpaḥ ||
                        vaktākāsamavitaralālpakaṇṭakavṛkṣavarṣaprasravaṇodapānaprāyoṣṇadārūṇavātapraviralālpaśailasthirakṛśaśarīramanuṣyaprāyo
                        vātapittaro gabhūyiṣṭhaś ca jāṅgalaḥ | ubhayalakṣaṇas sādhāraṇasya
                        pradhāna iti || bha || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.43"><label>1.35.43</label> samāḥ sādhāraṇe yasmād

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.45"/>

                        <caesura/>
                         sampattau bheṣajādīnām valasatvāyuṣān tathā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.47"><label>1.35.47</label> kevalaḥ samadehāgneḥ
                        sukhasādhyatamo mataḥ |
                        <caesura/>

                        <caesura/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.35.44"><label>1.35.44</label> na tathā balavantaḥ syuḥ

                <div n="36" type="adhyāya" corresp="1.37 in NAK 5-333">



                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.1"><label>1.36.1</label> athāto
                        bhūmipravibhāgavijñānīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.3"><label>1.36.3</label>
                        svabhraśarkkarāśmaviṣamavalmīkaśmaśānāghatadevatāyatanasikatoṣairar
                        anupahatāmanūṣarāmabhaṃgurāmadūrodakāṃ snigdhāṃ prarohavatīṃ
                        mṛdvīṃ sthirāṃ samāṃ gaurīṃ lohitāṃ vā bhūmim auṣadha grahaṇāya
                        parīkṣeta || tasyāṅ jātam api hi
                        krimaviṣaśastrātapapavanadahanatoyasambādhamārggair
                        anupahatamekasāraṃ puṣṭam avagāḍhamūlaṃ cauṣadhamādadyād ity eṣāṃ
                        bhūmiparīkṣāvibhāgaḥ sāmānyaḥ | || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.4"><label>1.36.4</label> viśeṣatas tu tatra
                        aśmavatī sthirā gurvvī śdhāmā kṛṣṇā vā sthūlatṛṇaśasyaprāyāḥ
                        svaguṇabhūyiṣṭhā | snigdhā śītalāsannodakā
                        snigdhatṛṇaśasyākomalavṛkṣaprāyā śuklāmbuguṇabhūyiṣṭhā ||
                        nānāvarṇṇā laghvāśmavatī viralālyapāṇḍuraprarohāgniguṇabhūyiṣṭhā
                        || rūkṣā bhasmarāsabhavarṇṇā
                        kṣatanuvṛkṣakoṭarālparasaprāyānilaguṇabhūyiṣṭhā || mṛdvī
                        samāvyabhravatyavyaktarasajalā mahāparvvatavṛkṣaprāryā syāmā
                        cākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhā || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.5"><label>1.36.5</label> tatra kecid ācāryāḥ
                        prāvṛṭvarṣāśaraddhemantavasantagrīṣmeṣu yathāsaṃkhyam
                        mūlapattratvacakṣīrasāraphalāny ādadīta || tat tu na samyak kasmāt
                        saumyāgneyatvāj jagataḥ | saumyāny auṣadhāni saumyeṣv ṛtuṣv
                        ādadīta | āgneyāny āgneyeṣv evam avyāpannāni bhavanti || saumyāny
                        auṣadhāni saumyeṣv ṛtuṣu gṛhītāni somaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ bhūmau
                        madhuratarāsnigdhatarāṇiśītatarāṇi bhavanti | </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.5a"><label>1.36.5a</label> āgneyāny auṣadhāni
                        āgneyeṣv ṛtuṣu gṛhītānyagniguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ bhūmau uṣṇatarāṇi
                        kaṭutarāṇi rūkṣatarāṇi bhavanti | </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.6"><label>1.36.6</label> tatrā
                        pṛthivῑguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ bhūmau jātāni virecanadravyāṇyādadīta |
                        agnyanilaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāñ ca vamanadravyāṇi |
                        ubhayaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyām ubhayatobhāgaharāṇi | ākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ
                        saṃśamanāny evam balavattarāṇi bhavanti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.36.7"><label>1.36.7</label> sarvvāṇi cābhinavānyatra
                        madhughṛtapippalīviḍaṅgebhya iti || </l>

                <div n="38" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 38, draft based on MS H]</head>





                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.1"><label>1.38.1</label>athāto dravyasaṅgrahaṇīyam
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.3"><label>1.38.3</label>pañcatriṃśad dravyagaṇā
                        bhavanti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.38.4"><label>1.38.4</label>tad yathā | vidārigandhā
                        vidārīviśvadevā sahadevāśvadaṃṣṭrā pṛthakparṇṇī śatāvarīe śārivā
                        jīvakarṣabho kṣudrasahā bṛhatyau
                        punarnnaiveraṇḍahaṃsapādīvṛścikālyṛṣabhī śṛgālavinnā ceti ||</l>

                <div n="40" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 40, draft based on MS H]</head>




                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.1"><label>1.40.1</label> athāto
                        dravyarasavīryavipākavijñānīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.2"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.3"><label>1.40.3</label> kecid ācāryā vruvate |
                        dravyam pradhānam kasmāt vyavasthitatvāt | iha khalu dravyam
                        vyavasthitanna rasādayaḥ | yathā ye phale rasādayas te pakve na
                        bhavanti || nityatvāc ca nityaṃ hi dravyamanityaṃ hi guṇāḥ | yathā
                        kalkādi pravibhāgās tad eva sampannarasagandhaṃ
                        vyāpannarasagandhavān bhavatīti | svajātivyavasthānāc ca yathā
                        pārthivaṃ dravyam anyabhāvan na gacchati | evaṃ śoṣāṇi |
                        pañcendriyagrahaṇāc ca | pañcaindriyair gṛhyate draṣṭavyanna
                        rasādayaḥ | āśrayatvāc ca dravyam āśritārasā iti | ārambha
                        sāmarthyāc ca dravyāśrita ārambhaḥ || yathā vidārigandhādim
                        āhṛtyāvadya vipaced ity evam ādiṣu na rasādiṣ ārambhaḥ |
                        śāstraprāmāṇyāc ca śāstraṃ ha | dvividhan dravyaṃ
                        sthāvarañjañgamti | kramāpekṣikatvāc ca rasādīnāṃ rasādayo hi
                        dravyakramam apekṣante yathā taruṇe taruṇāḥ | saṃpūrṇa sampūrṇā
                        iti | ekadeśasādhyatvāc ca dravyāṇām ekadeśenāpi vyādhayaḥ
                        sādhyante | yathā mahāvṛkṣakṣīreṇeti | tasmād dravyam pradhānan
                        rasādayaḥ kasmāt niravayavatvāt dravyasya | dravyalakṣaṇan tu
                        kriyāguṇasamavāyaḥ kriyādravye vidyate | guṇāḥ samavāyakāraṇañceti
                        ||</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.4"><label>1.40.4</label> netyāhur anye rasās tu
                        pradhānan kasmāt āgamāt āgamo hi śāstram ity ucyate | śāstre rasā
                        adhikṛtā yathā rasāyatta āhāra iti | upadeśāc ca | upadiśyate hi |
                        yathā madhurāmlalavaṇā vātaṃ śamayanti | ato rasāḥ pradhānaṃ |
                        anumāc ca | rasato hy anumīyate dravyaṃ | yathā madhuram iti ||
                        ṛṣivacanāc ca | ṛṣivacano vedaḥ | yathā kiñcidījyārtham
                        madhuramāhared iti | tasmāt rasāḥ pradhānaṃ | raseṣu tu guṇasaṃjñā
                        rasalakṣaṇam atro padekṣyāmaḥ | </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.5"><label>1.40.5</label> netyāhur anye vīryam
                        pradhānam iti | kasmāt prādhānyāt | ihatvauṣadhakarmmāṇi vīrya
                        prādhānyaṃ na bhavanti | tad yathā |
                        urddhabhāgodhobhāgobhayabhāgasaṃśamanaṃ
                        sāṅgrāhikadīpanalekhanavṛṃhaṇarasāyanavājīkaraṇaś ca
                        yathuharavilayanadāraṇamarddanaprāṇaghnaviṣapraśamanāni vīrya
                        prādhānyena bhavanti | tantu vīryaṃ dvividhaṃ | uṣṇaṃ śītaṃ
                        cāgniṣomīyatvāj jagataḥ | kecid aṣṭavidham āhuḥ | uṣṇaṃ śītaṃ
                        snigdhaṃ rūkṣam vi ṣadam piccilam mṛdus tīkṣṇañ ceti | etāni khalu
                        vīryāṇi svabhāvaguṇotkarṣād rasam abhibhūyātmakarmma kurvvanti |
                        yathā tāvad vṛhatyañ ca mūlaṅ kaṣāya tiktaṃ vātaṃ śamayaty
                        uṣṇavīryatvāt | kaṭukā pippalīpittaṃ śamayati | mṛduśītavīryatvāt
                        | tiktā kākamācī pittaṃ varddhayaty uṣṇavīryatvāt | kaṭukaṃ mūlaṃ
                        śleṣmāṇaṃ varddhayati snigdhavīryatvāt | amlaṃ kapitthaṃ śleṣmāṇaṃ
                        ti rukṣavīryatvāt || bha || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.6"><label>1.40.6</label> ye rasā vātaśamanā
                        bhavanti yadi teṣu vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         rukṣalāghavaśaity āni na te hanyuḥ samīraṇam || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.7"><label>1.40.7</label> ye rasāḥ pittaśamanā
                        bhavanti yadi teṣuvai |
                        <caesura/>
                         taikṣṇyauṣṇyalaghutā caiva na te talkarmmakāriṇaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.8"><label>1.40.8</label> ye rasāḥ śleṣmaśamanā
                        bhavanti yadi teṣu vai |
                        <caesura/>
                         snehagauravaśaity ānu na te tatkarmmakāriṇaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.9"><label>1.40.9</label> tasmād vīryaṃ pradhānam
                        iti || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.10"><label>1.40.10</label> netyāhur anye vipākaḥ
                        pradhānam iti | kasmāt samyaṅ mithyā vipakvatvāt | iha hi
                        dravyāṇyapaha tāni samyaṅ mithyā cāvipakvāni guṇan doṣam vā
                        janayaṃti | tatrāhur anye prati ra sampāka iti | vipākaḥ kecit
                        trividham icchanti | madhuram amlam kaṭukañceti | tat tu na samyak
                        | bhūtaguṇādāgamāc cāmlo vipāko nāsti | pittaṃ hi vidagdham
                        amlatām upaity āgneyatvāt | yad evaṃ lavaṇo 'pyanyaḥ pāke
                        bhaviṣyati | śleṣmā hi vidagdho lavaṇatām upaiti | tamādasiddhānta
                        eṣaḥ | pratirasam amlāmlasyaivaṃ sarvvaṣām iti dṛṣṭāntañ
                        codāharanti | yathā śāliyavamudgādayaḥ prakīrṇāḥ svabhāvam
                        uttarakāle pi na parity ajanti tadvat iti | kecit punar avalavanto
                        valavatāṃ vaśamāyānt it evam avasthitaḥ pāka iti | āgame svāha |
                        dvividha eva pāko madhuraḥ kaṭukaś ca | tayor madhurākhyo guruḥ
                        kaṭukākhyo laghur iti | tatra pṛthivyaptejovāyvākāśānāṃ
                        dvaividhyam bhavati | guṇasādharmyāngurutā | laghutā ca pṛthivyā
                        yo gurvyaḥ | śeṣāṇi laghūni tasmād dvividha eva pāko bhavati ||
                        bha ||</l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.11"><label>1.40.11</label> dravyeṣu pacyamāneṣu
                        yeṣv amvupṛthivīguṇāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         nivarttante 'dhikās tatra pāko madhura ucyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.12"><label>1.40.12</label> tejonilākāśaguṇāḥ
                        pacyamāneṣu yeṣu tu |
                        <caesura/>
                         nivarttante 'dhikās tatra pākaḥ kaṭuka ucyate || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.13"><label>1.40.13</label> pṛthak tvavādināmeṣeva
                        vādinām vādasaṃgrahaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         caturṇṇām api sāmagryam icchantyatra vipaścitaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.14"><label>1.40.14</label> tad dravyam ātmanā
                        kiñcit kiñcid vīryeṇa sevitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kiñcid rasavipākābhyān doṣaṃ hanti karoti vā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.15"><label>1.40.15</label> pāko nāsti vinā vīryād
                        vīryan nāsti vinā rasāt |
                        <caesura/>
                         raso nāsti vinā dravyād dravyaṃ śreṣṭhatamaṃ smṛtaṃ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.16"><label>1.40.16</label> janman tu dravyarasayor
                        anyonyāpekṣikaṃ smṛtaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         anyonyāpekṣikaṃ janma yathā syād dehadehinoḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.17"><label>1.40.17</label> vīryasaṃjñā guṇā ye
                        'ṣṭau te 'pi dravyāśrayāḥ smṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         raseṣu na bhavantyete nirguṇāḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.18"><label>1.40.18</label> dravye dravye ca
                        yasmāddhi vipacyante na ṣaḍ rasāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śreṣṭhaṃ dravyamato jñeyaṃ śeṣā bhāvās tadāśrayāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.19"><label>1.40.19</label> amīmāṃsyānyacintyāni
                        prasiddhāni svabhāvataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āgamenopayojyāni bheṣajāni vicakṣaṇaiḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.20"><label>1.40.20</label> pratyakṣalakṣaṇaphalās
                        prasiddhāś ca svabhāvataḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         oṣadhīn hetubhir vvidvān na parīkṣet kathañcana || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.21"><label>1.40.21</label> sahastreṇāpi hetūnān
                        nāmvaṣṭhādir virecayet |
                        <caesura/>
                         tasmāt tiṣṭhed vimatimānāgameśa tu hetuṣu || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.22"><label>1.40.22</label> yā svabhāvavijñānaṃ vā
                        raśaṃ yuktasenikaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         āturopakramam miśraṃ bhūmijñānan tathaiva ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.40.23"><label>1.40.23</label> dravyasaṃgrahaṇañcaiva
                        tathā śamanaśodhanaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         rasavīryavipākena proktam anyaddaśaiva tu || || </l>

                    <p ana="trailer"> caturthodaśa || || || </p>


                </div>

                <div n="41" type="adhyāya">
                    <head>[Adhyāya 41]</head>
                    <p xml:lang="en">[First draft based on MS N]</p>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.1"><label>1.41.1</label> athāto
                        dravyaviśeṣavijñānīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.3"><label>1.41.3</label> tatra
                        pṛthivyaptejovāyvākāśānāṃ samudāyād dravyābhinirvṛttir bbhavati |
                        idaṃ pārthivam idam apyam idan tejasam idam vāyavyam idam ākāśyam
                        iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.1"><label>1.41.4.1</label> tatra
                        sthūlasāndramandasthiragurukaṭhinagaṃdhaguṇabahulam
                        īṣatkaṣāyaprāyaso madhuram iti pārthivan tat
                        sthairyagauravasaṃghātopacayakaraṃ viśeṣataś cādhogatisvabhāvam
                        iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.2"><label>1.41.4.2</label>
                        śītastimitamandagururasasāndramṛdupicchilarasaguṇarasaguṇabahulam
                        īṣadamlaṃ prāyaso madhuram āpyan tat snehanahlādanaviṣyandanakaram
                        iti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.3"><label>1.41.4.3</label>
                        tīkṣṇoṣṇarūkṣasūkṣmalaghuviṣadaṃ rūpaguṇabahulam īṣadamlaprāyam
                        viśeṣataś corddhvagatisvabhāvam iti taijasaṃ ||
                        taddahanapacanatāpanaprakāśanaprabhāvarṇṇakaram iti | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.4"><label>1.41.4.4</label>
                        sūkṣmarūkṣakharaśiśiralaghuviṣadaṃ sparśaguṇabahulam īṣattiktam
                        viśeṣataḥ kaṣāyam iti vāyavyaṃ tadvaiṣadyaṃ
                        lāghavaglapanavirūkṣaṇakaram iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.5"><label>1.41.4.5</label>
                        ślakṣṇasūkṣmavyavāyiviṣadaviviktarasaṃ śabdaguṇabahulam ākāśyan
                        tasmāt tat mārddavasauṣiryalāghavakaram iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.5"><label>1.41.5</label> anena nidarśanena
                        nānauṣadhabhūtañ jagati kiñcid dravyam astīti kṛtvā tan taṃ
                        yuktiviśeṣamarthañ cābhipratītya svavīryaguṇayuktāni dravyāṇi
                            kārmmukāni<anchor n="SS.1.41.5-n1"/> bhavanti || tāni yadā
                        kurvvanti sa kālaḥ | yat kurvanti tat karmma | yena kurvvanti tad
                        vīryaṃ | yatra kurvvanti tad adhikaraṇaṃ | yathā kurvvanti sa
                        upāyaḥ | yad abhiniṣpādayanti tat phalam iti | </l>

                    <ab corresp="#SS.1.41.5" type="apparatus">
                        <list type="notes">
                            <item corresp="#SS.1.41.5-n1">The word
                                    "<foreign>kārmuka</foreign>" for "effective" is very
                                rare, apparently only known from this instance and one in
                                the Carakasaṃhitā 1.26.13. The word is formed by P.5.1.103
                                and the grammatical Kāśikāvṛtti says that it is confined
                                to describing a "capable" bow since no other usage of the
                                word is known.</item>
                        </list>
                    </ab>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.6"><label>1.41.6</label> tad atra virecanadravyāṇy
                        ambupṛthivīguṇabhūyiṣṭhāni | pṛthivyāpo hi gurvvyaḥ | gurutvād
                        adho gacchanti | tasmād virecanadravyāṇy
                        ambupṛthivīguṇabhūyiṣṭhāni | vamanadravyāṇy
                        agnivāyuguṇabhūyiṣṭhāni | agnivāyū hi laghū laghutvāc corddhvam
                        uttiṣṭhataḥ | tasmād vamanaprāmāṇyād agnivāyubhūyiṣṭhāny
                        ubhayaguṇabhūyiṣṭhan dravyam ubhayato bhāgaharaṃ |
                        ākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ saṃśamanaṃ | sāṃgrāhikam anilaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ |
                        dīpanam agniguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ | lekhanam anilānalaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ |
                        bṛṃhanam pṛthivyambuguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ | evam auṣadhakarmmāṇy anumānāt
                        sādhayet || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.7"><label>1.41.7</label> bhavanti ślokāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.7i"><label>1.41.7i</label> mahyambvagnyātmakair
                        ddravyais tribhiḥ sāmyati mārutaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         khabhūmyambuvāyujaiḥ pittañ caturbbhiḥ saṃpraśāmyati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.8"><label>1.41.8</label> kaphaḥ khatejo'nilajais
                        tribhiḥ śāmyati dehināṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         khavāyuktābhyān dravyābhyāṃ vṛddhim abhyeti mārutaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.9"><label>1.41.9</label> āgneyam eva yad dravyan
                        tena pittam udīryate |
                        <caesura/>
                         mahyambujābhyān dravyābhyāṅ kaphaś cābhivivarddhate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.10"><label>1.41.10</label> evam eva guṇādhikyaṃ
                        dravye dravye vyavasthitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         dviśo vā bahuśo vāpi jñātvā doṣe 'vacācaret || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.11"><label>1.41.11</label> tatra ya ime
                        guṇāṣṭauvīryasaṃjñakāḥ |
                        śītoṣṇasnigdharūkṣamṛdutīkṣṇapicchilaviṣadās teṣān tīkṣṇoṣṇāv
                        āgneyau | śītapicchilāv ambuguṇabhūyiṣṭhau |
                        pṛthivīsomaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaḥ | snehas toyākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ |
                        mṛdutvaṃ | vāyuguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ raukṣyaṃ | kṣitisamīraṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ
                        vaiṣadyaṃ | vipākāv uktaguṇau | karmmāṇy uṣṇasya
                        dahanapācanamūrcchanasvedanavamanavirecanāni || śītasya
                        prahlādanaviṣkambhanasthirīkaraṇaprasādanakledanajīvanāni |
                        snigdhasya snehanabṛṃhaṇasantarppaṇavyājīkaraṇavayaḥsthāpanāni ||
                        rūkṣasyānilavṛddhisaṃgrahaṇapīḍanavirūkṣaśoṣarohaṇāni || viṣadasya
                        kledāvūṣaṇavirūkṣaśoṣarohaṇāni ||
                        picchilasyopalepanapūraṇabṛṃhaṇasaṃśleṣaṇavyājīkaraṇāni || mṛdo
                        raktamān saprasādanamukhyasaṃsparśanāni || tīkṣṇasya
                        saṅgrahācūṣaṇāvadāraṇaśrāvaṇāni | tatroṣṇasnigdhau vātaghnau |
                        śītamṛdupicchilāḥ pittaghnāḥ | tīkṣṇarūkṣaviṣadāḥ śleṣmaghnāḥ |
                        gurupāko vātapittaghnaḥ | laghupākaḥ śleṣmapittaghna iti | teṣu
                        mṛduśītoṣṇāḥ sparśagrāhyāḥ | picchilaviṣadau cakṣuḥsparśābhyāṃ |
                        snigdharūkṣau cakṣuṣā | tīkṣṇaḥ sukhaduḥkhotpādanāt | gurupākaḥ
                        sṛṣṭaviṇmūtratayā kaphāṃ kleśanañ ca | laghur bbaddhaviṇmūtratayā
                        mārutakopanañ ca | tatra tulyaguṇeṣu bhūteṣu rasavaiśeṣyam
                        upalakṣayet || yathā madhuro guruś ca pārthivaḥ |
                        madhurasnigdhaśītāś cāpyā iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.12"><label>1.41.12</label> || bhavati cātra || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.41.12i"><label>1.41.12i</label> guṇā ye uktā dravyeṣu
                        śarīreṣv api tān viduḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sthānavṛddhikṣayāt tasmād dehināṃ dravyahetukā iti || </l>

                <div n="42" type="adhyāya">
                    <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 42, draft based on MS H]</head>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.1"><label>1.42.1</label> athāto
                        rasaviśeṣavi-jñānīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.2"><label>1.42.2</label>
                    </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.3"><label>1.42.3</label>
                        ākāśapavanadahanatoyabhūmiṣu yathāsaṅkhyam ekottaraparivṛddhāḥ ||
                        śa bdasparśarūparasagandhāḥ || tasmād āpyo rasaḥ
                        parasparānupraveśāc ca sarvveṣāṃ sānnidhyam asti utkarṣāt tu
                        grahaṇaṃ | sa khalvāpyo rasaḥ śeṣabhūtasaṃsarggādvidagdhaḥ
                        ṣaḍvidho bhavati | tad yathā | madhuro 'mlo lavaṇaḥ kaṭukastiktaḥ
                        kaṣāya iti | tatrodakavāhulyātmadhuraḥ | toyāgnivāhulyādamlaḥ
                        bhūmyagnivāhulyāl lavaṇaḥ vāyvākāśavāhulyāttiktaḥ |
                        vāyvagnivāhulyātkaṭukaḥ pṛthivyanilavāhulyātkaṣāya iti || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.4"><label>1.42.4</label> tatra madhurāmlalavaṇā
                        vātaghnāḥ | madhuratiktakaṣāyāḥ pittaghnāḥ kaṭutiktakaṣāyāḥ
                        śleṣmaghnāḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.5"><label>1.42.5</label> tatra vāyurātmaivātmā |
                        pittamāgneyaṃ | śleṣma saumya iti || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.6"><label>1.42.6</label> ta ete rasāḥ
                        svayonivardhanā anyayonipraśamanāś ca | </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.7"><label>1.42.7</label> kecid āhur
                        agnīṣomīyatvājjagataḥ | dvividhā rasāḥ saumyā āgneyāś ca | tatra
                        madhuratiktakaṣāyāḥ saumyāḥ dvividhā kaṭvamlalavaṇā āgneyāḥ |
                        madhurāmlalavaṇāḥ snigdhā guravaś ca dvividhā kaṭutiktakaṣāyā
                        rūkṣā laghavaś ca | saumyāḥ śītāḥ | āgneyās tūṣṇāḥ | </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8.1"><label>1.42.8.1</label> tatra
                            śaityarūkṣalāghavavaiṣadyaguṇala<cb n="2"/>kṣaṇo vāyuḥ | tasya
                        samānayoniḥ kaṣāyo rasaḥ | saumyaḥ śaityāc chaity am
                        abhivardhayati | raukṣyād raukṣyaṃ lāghavāl lāghavaṃ vaiṣadyād
                        vaiṣadyam iti || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8.2"><label>1.42.8.2</label>
                            auṣṇyataikṣṇyaraukṣyalāghavavaiṣa<cb n="2"
                        />dyaguṇalakṣaṇampittantasya samānayoniḥ kaṭuko rasaḥ | saumya
                        auṣṇyād auṣṇyam abhivardhayati | taikṣṇyāt taikṣṇyaṃ raukṣyād
                        raukṣyaṃ lāghavāl lāghavaṃ vaiśadyād vaiśadyam iti || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8.3"><label>1.42.8.3</label>
                        mādhuryasnehagauravaśaityapaicchilyaguṇalakṣaṇaḥ śleṣmā tasya
                        samānayo nirmadhuro rasaḥ | saumya mādhuryāt mādhuryam
                        abhivardhayati | snehāt snehaṃ gauravād gauravaṃ śaityāc chaityaṃ
                        paicchilyāt paicchilyam iti ||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8"><label>1.42.8</label>tasya punar vviparītaḥ
                        kaṭuko rasaḥ | śleṣmaṇaḥ pratyanīkatvāt | kaṭukyātmādhuryam
                        abhibhavati | raukṣyāt snehaṃ lāghavād gauravaṃ auṣṇyāt paicchity
                        an tad etan nidarśanamātram uktaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.9"><label>1.42.9</label> rasalakṣaṇam ata ūrdhvaṃ
                        vakṣyāmaḥ || tatra yaḥ paritoṣam utpādayati tarppayati
                        mukhopalepañ janayati prahlādayati śleṣmāṇañ cābhivardhayati sa
                        madhuraḥ || yo dantaharṣam utpādayati | mukhāśrāvañ jana-yati
                        śraddhāñ cotpādayati so 'mlaḥ || yo bhaktarucim utpādayati |
                        kaphaprasekañ janayati mārddavañ copādayati sa lavaṇaḥ || yo
                        jihvām udvejayati śiro gṛhṇāti nāsikāñ ca śrāvayati sa kaṭukaḥ ||
                        yo gale śoṣam utpāda-yati mukhavaiṣadyam utpādayati bhaktaruciñ
                        copādyati sa tiktaḥ || ya āsyam pariśoṣayati- jihvāṃ stambhayati
                        kaṇṭham badhnāti hṛdayam pīḍayati sa kaṣāyaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.1"><label>1.42.10.1</label> rasaguṇān ata
                        ūrdhvam vakṣyāmaḥ || tatra madhuro raso raktamāṃsado 'sthimajjojaḥ
                        śukravardhanaś cākṣuṣyaḥ keśyauvalakṛtsandhānaḥ śoṇitaḥ
                        śoṇitaprasādo vālavṛddhakṣatakṣīṇahitaḥ
                        ṣaṭpadapipīlikānāmiṣṭatamaḥ || tṛṣṇāmūrcchādāhaḥ praśamanaḥ |
                        ṣaḍindriyaprasādanaś ceti | sa evaṃguṇo 'py eka evātyartham
                        upayujyamānaḥ kāsaḥ śvāso
                        lasakavamathurvvadanamādhuryasvaropaghātakṛmigalagaṇḍān āpādayati
                        | tathārvvudaślīpadavastigudopalepābhiṣyandaprabhṛtīn
                        nayanavikārānn upajayati || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.2"><label>1.42.10.2</label> amlas tu jaraṇaḥ
                            pācanapavana<cb n="2"/>nigrahaṇo nulomano vidāhī vahiḥśītaḥ
                        kledanaḥ prāyaśo hṛdyaś ceti | sa khalv evaṃguṇo 'py eka
                        evātyartham upayujyamāno dantaharṣanayanasammīlanaro<cb n="2"
                        />masamvejanakaphavilāyanaśarīrapraśithilatām āpādayati | tathā
                        kṣatavihatadagdhadaṣṭabhagnaśū-nacyutāvamathitacchiyavisarppitacchinnaviddhotpiṣṭādīni
                            pāca-<cb n="2"/>yaty āgneyasvabhāvatvvāt || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.3"><label>1.42.10.3</label> lavaṇas tu
                        saṃśodhanaḥ pācano viśleṣaṇas tarppaṇaḥ kledanaḥ śaithilyakṛt
                        sarvvarasapratyanīkabhūto mārggaviśodhanaḥ sarvvaśarīrāvayavamā<cb
                            n="2"/>rddavakaraś ceti | sa khalu evaṃguṇo 'py eka
                        evātyartham upasevyamāno gātrakaṇḍūko tha śophavaivarṇṇakaraḥ
                        svaropaghātendriyopatāpān upajanayati |
                        tathākṣimukhapākaraktapittavātaśoṇitāmlīkāprabhṛtīnvikārān
                        upajanayati || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.4"><label>1.42.10.4</label> kaṭukas tu dīpanaḥ
                        pācano rocanaḥ śodhanaḥ sthaulyā
                        lyālasakaviṣakuṣṭhakaṇḍūpraśamanaḥ sandhibandhacchedano vasādanas
                        stanyaśukrakaphamedasām upahantā ceti | sa khalv evaṃguṇo 'py eka
                        evātyartham upayujyamāno bhramamadagalatālvoṣṭhaśoṣadāhasantāpān
                        āpādayati | <cb n="2"/>tathā valavighātakampatodabhedakṛt
                        karacaraṇapārśvapṛṣṭhaprabhṛtiṣu ca vātaśūlān upajanayati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.5"><label>1.42.10.5</label> tiktas tu rocano
                        dīpanaḥ śodhanaḥ kaṇḍūkoṣṭhatṛṣṇāmūrcchāpraśanaḥ stanyaśodhano
                        viṇmūtrakledamedovasāpūyopaśoṣaṇaś ceti | sa khalv evaṅguṇo 'py
                        eka evātyartham upayujyamāno
                        gātramanyāstambhākṣepakordditaśiraḥśūlān upa-janayati | tathā
                        bhramatodabhedacchedāsyavairasyāny āpādayati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.6"><label>1.42.10.6</label>kaṣāyas tu saṅgrāhiko
                        ropaṇaḥ stambhanaḥ śodhanollekhanaḥ śoṣaṇaḥ pīḍanaḥ kledopaśoṣaṇaś
                        ceti | sa khalv evaṅguṇo 'py eka evātyartham upayujyamāno
                        hṛdayapīḍāsyaśoṣodarādhmānavākyagrahamanyāstambhaprabhṛtīn vikārān
                        upajanayati | tathā
                        gātrasphuraṇacimicimāyanākuñcanākṣepaṇaprabhṛtīn
                        vikārānupajanayati || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.11"><label>1.42.11</label> sarvveṣām eva dravyāṇy
                        upadekṣyāmaḥ | tad yathā kākolyādi
                        kṣīraghṛtavasāmajjaśāliyavagodhūmamāṣaśṛṅgāṭakakaśeruka
                        kālāṅkālukapiyālapuṣkaravījakāśmaryamadhūkadrākṣākharjūrarājādananālikerekṣuvikārāḥ
                        | balātibalātmaguptāvidārīpayasyā<cb n="2"
                        />gokṣurakakṣīramoraṭamadhūlikākūṣmāṇḍādiḥ samāsena madhuro
                        varggaḥ ||
                            dāḍimāmalakamātuluṅgāmrāmrātakakapitthakaramarddavadaraprācīnāmalakakośā<cb
                            n="2"
                        />mrabhavyapārāvatavetraphalatintiḍīkalajacāmlavetasadantaśaṭhadadhitakrasurāsauvīratuṣodakadhānyāmlaprabhṛtīni
                        samāsenāmlo varggaḥ || saindhavasauvarccalavi-<cb n="2"
                        />ḍapākyaromakasāmudrapācimakṣāroṣarasuvarccilaprabhṛtīni samāsena
                        lavaṇo varggaḥ || pippa-lyādiḥ surasādir
                            mmadhuśigrumūlakalaśunasumukhaśītaśi<cb n="2"
                        />vakuṣṭhadevadāruhareṇukā
                        'valgujaphalacaṇḍāguggulumustalāṅgalakīśukanāsīpīluprabhṛtī-ni
                        śālasārādiś ca prāyaśaḥ kaṭuko varggaḥ ||
                        āragvadhādirgguḍūcyādirmmaṇḍūkaparṇṇīvetrakarīraharidrādvayendrayavavaruṇasvādukaṇṭakasaptaparṇṇavṛhatīdvayaśaṃkhinītṛvṛtkṛtavedhanakarkkoṭakakāravellavārttākukaravīrasumanāḥśaṃkhapuṣpyapāmārggatrāyamāṇāśokarohivaijayantīsuvarccalāvṛścikālījyotiṣmatīprabhṛtīni
                        tikto varggaḥ || nyagrodhādirambaṣṭhādir lodhrādiḥ
                        priyaṅvādistriphalā śallakījamvvasthitindukādīni katakaśākaphalāni
                        sālasārādiś ca prāyasaḥ
                        kuravakakovidārajīvantīsuniṣaṇṇakaprabhṛtīni varakādayo mudgādayaś
                        ca samāsena kaṣā-yo varggaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.12"><label>1.42.12</label> tatraiteṣāṃ rasānāṃ
                        saṃyogās triṣaṣṭirv bhavanti || tad yathā pañcadaśa dvikāḥ |
                        viṃśatis trikāḥ | pañcadaśa catuṣkāḥ | ṣaṭ pañcakāḥ | ekaṣaṭkāḥ |
                        ekaikaśaś ca śaḍrasā iti | teṣām anyatra vakṣyāmaḥ || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.42.13"><label>1.42.13</label> bhavati cātra || yuktāḥ
                        ṣaḍadhigacchanti valino vaśyatāṃ rasāḥ | yathā doṣāḥ prakupitā
                        vaśaṃ yānti valīyasa iti ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.1"><label>1.43.1</label> athāto
                        vamanadravyavikalpavijñānīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.2"/>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3a"><label>1.43.3a</label> vamanadravyānām
                        phalākhyānām madhye madanaphalāni śreṣṭhatamāni bhavanti || tatra
                        madanapuṣpāṇām ātapaśuṣkāṇā cūrṇaprakuñcaṃ pratyak
                        puṣpīnimvakaṣāyāṇām anyatamenālo pāyayitvā vāmayet |
                        madanaśatvāṭūcūrṇṇāny evam madhulavaṇayuktāny abhiprataptāni |
                        madanaśalāṭucūrṇṇasiddhām vā tilayavāgūn | nivṛttām vā nātihariti
                        pāṇḍūnāṃ kuśamūḍhāvavaddhamṛdgomayapraliptānāṃ
                        yavavūsamāṣaśālyādidhānyarāśāvaṣṭharātroṣitaklinnabhinnānām
                        phalapippalīrāhṛtyātape pariśoṣayet tāsāṃ
                        dadhipalavimṛditapariśuṣkāṇāṃ subhājanasthānām antarnnakhamuṣṭhim
                        uṣṇena yaṣṭhīmadhukaṣāyeṇa kovidārādhyanyatamakāṣāyeṇa vā vimṛdya
                        trirātraparyuṣitam madhusaindhavayuktam āśīrbhir abhimantritam
                        udaṅmukhaḥ prāṅmukham āturam pāyayet anena mantreṇa abhimantrya
                        ||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3.1"
                        ><label>1.43.3.1</label>brahmadakṣāśvirūdrendrabhūcandrārkkānilānalāḥ
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         ṛṣayaḥ sauṣadhigrāmā bhūtasaṃghāś ca pāntu te || </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3.2"><label>1.43.3.2</label>rasāyaneva siddhānān
                        devānām amṛtaṃ yathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         sudhevottamanāgānāsbhaiṣajyam idam astu te ||</l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3b"><label>1.43.3b</label>viśeṣeṇa
                        śleṣmajvarapratiśyāyāntarvvidradhiṣv apravarttamāne doṣe
                        pippalīvacāsarṣapakalkonmiśrair uṣṇāmvubhiḥ punaḥ punaḥ
                        pravarttayed āsamyag vāntalakṣaṇād iti | madanaphalamajjacūrṇṇam
                        vā tatkvāthaparibhāvitam vasena dravyakaṣāyeṇa | madanaphalamajjā
                        siddham vā payaḥ | madanaphalamajjasiddhena vā payasā vā yavāgūm
                        adhobhāgāsṛhṛdrogayoḥ | madanaphalamajjasiddhasya vā payaso
                        dadhibhāvam upagatasya | dadhyuttarakaṃ dadhi vā
                        kaphaprasekaśarddistameṣu | madanaphalamajjācūrṇṇa rasam vā
                        bhallātakasenhavadādāya phāṇitībhūtaṃ lehayet | ātapaśuṣkam vā
                        jīvantī kaṣāyeṇa pittakaphasthānagate | madanaphala majjākvātham
                        vā pippalyādi prativāpaṃ ūṣaṇanimvakaṣāya yor anyatamena
                        santarppaṇaṃ | kaphasarvvavyādhiharam iti madanaphalam uktaṃ | </l>
                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.4"><label>1.43.4</label> jīmūtakakusumacūrṇṇam vā
                        pūrvvavad eva kṣīreṇa nivṛtteṣu yavāgūṃ romaseṣu | santānikām vā
                        nirllomaśeṣu | dadhyuttarakaṃ haritakapāṇḍuṣu | dadhi tat
                        kaṣāyasaṃsṛṭāṃ surām vā paryāgateṣu | madanaphalamajja </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.5"><label>1.43.5</label> vidhānavat
                        kuṭajaphalamajjavidhānaṃ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.6"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.7"><label>1.43.7</label> ikṣvākukusumacūrṇṇam vā
                        pūrvvavad eva kṣīreṇa | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.8"><label>1.43.8</label> dhāmārgavasyāpi
                        madanaphalamajjā vidhānavad upayogaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.43.9"><label>1.43.9</label>
                        kṛtavedhanamadanaphalamajjapippalīmām vamanadravyaparibhāvitānām
                        vahuśaś cūrṇṇam utpalādiṣu dattam āghrā ya vasati
                        tattvanavavaddhadoṣeṣu yavāgūmākaṇṭham pītavatsu ca dadyād iti |

                         suślakṣṇacūrṇṇitānīha gāḍitāni vimiśrayet ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.1"><label>1.45.1</label> athāto
                        dravadravyaviśeṣavijñānīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.2"/>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.3"><label>1.45.3</label> pānīyaṃm āntarīkṣyam
                        anirddeśyarasam amṛtaṃ jīvanan tarppaṇan dhāraṇam āśvāsajananaṃ
                        śramaklamapipāsāmadamūrcchātandrāpraśamanam ekāntataḥ pathyatamañ
                        ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.4"><label>1.45.4</label> tad evāvanau patitam
                        anyatamam upalabhyate |
                        nadīsarastaḍāgakūpavāpīpraśravaṇodbhijacauṇṭyādiṣu sthāneṣv
                        anyatamaṃ rasam upabhate | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.5"><label>1.45.5</label> tatra
                        lohitakapilapā-ṇḍupītanīlaśukleṣv avanipradeśeṣu
                        madhurāmlalavaṇakaṭutiktakaṣāyā yathāsaṃkhyam udakarasā bhavantīty
                        eke bhāṣante || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.6"><label>1.45.6</label> tat tu na samyak
                        pṛthivyādīnāmanyo 'nyānu-praveśakṛtaḥ sa khalūdakaraso
                        bhavatyutkarṣāpakarṣakṛtena saṃyogaviśeṣeṇa || tatra
                        svalakṣaṇodakaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyām madhuraṃ | toyāgniguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyām
                        amlaṃ| pṛthivyagniguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ lavaṇaṃ |
                        vāyvagniguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṅ kaṭukaṃ| vāyvākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ tiktaṃ
                        | pṛthivyanilaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṅ kaṣāyaṃ | ākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyām
                        avyaktarasam avyaktaṃ hy ākāśam ity atas tat pradhānam
                        avyaktarasatvāt tat peyam āntarīkṣālābhe | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.7"><label>1.45.7</label> tatrānta-rikṣañ
                        caturvvidhaṃ || tadyāthā | dhāraṃ kāraṃ tauṣāraṃ haimam iti |
                        teṣān dhāraṃ pradhānaṃ laghutvāt tat punar dvividhaṃ | gāṅgaṃ
                        sāmudrañ ca tayoḥ parīkṣaṇaṃ | tatra śālyodanapiṇḍam akuthitam
                        avidagdhaṃ | rajatabhājanopahitaṃ varṣati deve kurvvīta sa cet
                        muhūrttasthitas tādṛśa eva bhavati | tad gāṅgam iti avagantavyaṃ |
                        varṇṇānyatāsitthaprakledo vā tatsāmudram iti vidyāt | tan
                        nopādeyaṃ | sāmudram apy āśvayuji māsi gṛhītaṃ gāṅgavad bhavati |
                        tad upādeyam iti | śuklapaṭaikadeśapracyutam athavā
                        harmmyatalaparibhraṣṭam anyair vvā prayogair ggṛhītaṃ śailabhājane
                        śailavan mṛnmaye vā pātreṣv anuguptan nidadhyāt | tat sarvvakālam
                        upayuñjīta | tasyālābhe bhaumaṃ | tat punaḥ saptavidhaṃ | tad
                        yathā kaupan nādeyaṃ sārasan tāḍāga m prāsravaṇam audbhijaṃ
                        cauṇṭyam iti || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.8"><label>1.45.8</label> tatra
                        varṣāvarṣāsvāntarikṣamaudbhijaṃ vā seveta mahāguṇatvā-t | śaradi
                        sarvvam prasannatvāt | hemante sārasan tāḍāgam vā | vasante kaupaṃ
                        cauṇṭyaṃ prāsrāvaṇam vā | grīṣme 'pyevaṃ | prāvṛṣyendram
                        anabhivṛṣṭaṃ sarvvaṃ eva | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.9"><label>1.45.9</label>
                        kīṭamūtrapurīṣāṇḍaśava-kothapradūṣitaṃ | tṛṇaparṇṇodakayutaṃ
                        kaluṣam viṣasaṃyutaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.10"><label>1.45.10</label> yo 'vagāheta varṣāsu
                        pivedvāpi navañ jalaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sa vāhyābhyantarān rogān labhate kṣipram eva tu || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.45.11"><label>1.45.11</label> tatra yat
                        paṅkaśevālatṛṇahaṭhapadmaprabhṛtibhir avacchannaṃ
                        raviśaśikiraṇāni-lair vvātijuṣṭāṃ gandharasopasṛṣṭan tad vyāpannam
                        iti vidyāt | sparśarasarūpagandhavīryavipākāḥ | doṣāḥ ṣaṭ kharatā
                        paicchilyam auṣṇyaṃ dantagrāhitā ca sparśadoṣaḥ |
                        paṅkasikatāśaivālavāhulyādvikṛtavarṇṇatā rūpadoṣaḥ | vyaktarasatā
                        rasadoṣaḥ | aniṣṭagandhatā gandhadoṣaḥ | yad upayuktan
                        tṛṣṇāgauravaśūlakaphaprasekānā-pādayati sa vīryadoṣaḥ | yad
                        upayuktaṃ cirād vipacyate viṣṭambhayati sa vipākadoṣaḥ || ta ete
                        āntarikṣe doṣā na bhavanti | </l>

                        sādhāraṇatvāt | tatra sahyaprabhavāḥ kuṣṭhañ janayanti |
                        vindhyaprabhavā kuṣṭhaṃ hṛdrogañ ca | malayaprabhavāḥ krimīn |
                        mahendraprabhavāḥ ślīpadodarāṇi | himavatprabhavāḥ | galagaṇḍaṃ
                        kvacid gaṇḍamālāṃ | prācyāvanty āparāvantyāś cārśāṃsy upajanayanti
