                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.1"><label>1.46.1</label> athāto 'nnapānavidhim
                        vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.2"><label>1.46.2</label>
                    </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.3"><label>1.46.3</label> dhanvantarim abhivādya
                        suśruta uvāca || bhagavan prāgabhihitam prāṇināṃ mūlam āhāro
                        balavarṇṇaujasāñ ca saḥ ṣaṭsu raseṣv āyatto rasāḥ
                        punar dravyāśrayiṇaḥ | dravyarasavīryavipākanimitte ca kṣayavṛddhī
                        doṣāṇāṃ sātmyañ ca | brahmāder api ca lokasyāhāraḥ
                        sthityutpattihetur
                        āhārādevābhivṛddhir balam ārogyavarṇendriyaprasādaś ca | tathā
                        hy āhāravaiṣampādasvāsthyan tasyāsita<cb n="2"/>pītalīḍhakhāditasya
                        nānādravyātmakasyānekavidhavikalpaprabhāvasya pṛthak pṛthak
                        dravyarasavīryavipākakarmmecchāṃ jñātuṃ na hy
                        anavabuddhadravyasvabhāvā bhiṣajo roganigrahaṅ karttuṃ samarthā
                        ity āhārāyattāś ca prāṇino yasmāt tasmād annapānavidhim upadiśat tu
                        me bhagavān ity uktaḥ provāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ || atha khalu
                        vatsa suśruta || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.4"><label>1.46.4</label> tatra
                            lohitakaśālikalamakakarddamakapāṇḍukasugandhakasakunāhṛtakuṣmāṇḍakapuṇḍarīkamahāśāliśītabhīrukalodhraśūkadīrghaśūkakāñca<cb
                            n="2"/>nakahāyanakadūṣīmahākhyaprabhṛtayaḥ śālayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.5"><label>1.46.5</label> madhurā vīryataḥ śītā
                        vipākā kaṭukāḥ smṛtāḥ | pittaghnālpānilakaphaḥ snigdhā
                        vaddhālpavarccasaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.6"><label>1.46.6</label> teṣāṃ lohitakaḥ śreṣṭho
                        doṣaghnaḥ śukramūtralaḥ | cakṣuṣyo varṇṇavalakṛt svaryo hṛdyas
                        tṛṣāpahaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.7"><label>1.46.7</label> tasmād alpāntaraguṇāḥ
                        kramaśaḥ śālayo pare || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.8"><label>1.46.8</label>
                        ṣaṣṭikakāṅgakamukundakapītakapramodakakālakāsanapuṣpakamahāsvetakamahāvrīhicūrṇṇakakuravakedāraprabhṛtayo
                        vrīhayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.9"><label>1.46.9</label> rase pāke ca madhurāḥ
                        pittānilaharāḥ smṛtāḥ | śālīnāṅguṇataś cāpi samānā vaddhavarccasaḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.10"><label>1.46.10</label> ṣaṣṭikaḥ pravaras teṣāṅ
                        kaṣāyānuraso laghuḥ | mṛduḥ snigdhas tridoṣaghnaḥ
                        sthairyakṛdvalavarddhanaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.11"><label>1.46.11</label> rasato madhuragrāhī
                        tulyo lohitaśāli<cb n="2"/>bhiḥ | śeṣās tv alpāntarās tv asmād
                        vrīhayaḥ kramaśo guṇaiḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.12"><label>1.46.12</label>
                            kṛṣṇavrīhiśālāmukhalāvākṣajātumukhanandīmukhatvaritakakurkkuṭāṇḍakapārāvatakapāṭalāprabhṛ<cb
                            n="2"/>tayo vrīhayaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.13"><label>1.46.13</label> kaṣāyamadhurāḥ pāke
                        madhurā vīryato 'himāḥ | alpābhiṣyandinastulyāḥ ṣaṣṭikair
                        vvalavarddhanāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.14"><label>1.46.14</label> kṛṣṇavrīhirvvarasteṣāṃ
                        kaṣāyamadhuro laghuḥ | tasmād alpāntare guṇāḥ kramaśo vrīhayo
                        'pare || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.15"><label>1.46.15</label> dagdhāyāmavanau jātāḥ
                        śālayo laghupākinaḥ | kaṣāyā vaddhaviṇmūtrā rūkṣāḥ
                        śleṣmāpakarṣaṇāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.16"><label>1.46.16</label> sthalajāḥ
                        kaphapittaghnāḥ kaṣāyāḥ kaṭukānvayāḥ | kiñcitsatiktamadhurāḥ
                        pavanānalavarddhanāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.17"><label>1.46.17</label> kaidārā madhurā vṛṣyā
                        balyāḥ pittanivarhaṇāḥ | īṣatkaṣāyālpavalā guravaḥ kaphaśukralāḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.18"><label>1.46.18</label> ropyātiropyā laghavaḥ
                        śīghrapākā guṇottarāḥ | avidāhino vātaharā valyā mūtravivardha-nāḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.19"><label>1.46.19</label> śālayaś chinnarūḍhā ye
                        rūkṣā vaddhālpavarccasaḥ | tiktākaṣāyāḥ pittaghnā laghupākāḥ
                        kaphāpahāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.20"><label>1.46.20</label> vistareṇāyamuddiṣṭaḥ
                        śālivarggo hitāhitaḥ | tadvat kudhāny amudgānām māṣādīnāñ ca
                        vakṣyate || </l>





                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.21"><label>1.46.21</label>
                        koradūṣaśyāmākanīvāraśāntanuvarakoddālakapriyaṅgumadhūlikānandīmukhakuravindakasaka
                        varūkatolaparṇṇāmukundakaveṇuyavaprabhṛtayaḥ kudhānyaviśeṣāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.22"><label>1.46.22</label> uṣṇāḥ kaṣāyamadhurā
                        rūkṣāḥ kaṭuvipākinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śleṣmaghnā vātaniṣyandā vātapittaprakopanāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.23"><label>1.46.23</label> kaṣāyamadhūrāḥ
                        śītāsteṣāṃ pittasapāḥ smṛtāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         sakoradūṣaṇāmākonīraś caiva śāntanuḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.24"><label>1.46.24</label> kṛṣṇāraktāś ca pītāś ca
                        śvetāś caiva priyaṅgavaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         yathottaraṃ pradhānāḥ syūḥ snigdhāḥ kaphaharāḥ sarāḥ | </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.25"><label>1.46.25</label> madhūlī madhurāḥ śītāḥ
                        snigdhā nandīmukhī tathā |
                        <caesura/>
                         viśoṣī tatra bhūyiṣṭha varakaḥ samukundakaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.26"><label>1.46.26</label> rūkṣā veṇuyavā jñeyā
                        vīryoṣṇā kaṭupākinaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaddhamūtraḥ kaphaharāḥ kaṣāyā vātakopanāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.27"><label>1.46.27</label>
                        mudgavanamudgasūramukuṣṭhakalāyahareṇvāḍhakīsatīnā vaidalāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.28"><label>1.46.28</label> kaṣāyamadhurāḥ śītā
                        kaṭupākā nilāpahāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vaddhamūtrapurīṣāś ca pittaśleṣmaharās tathā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.29"><label>1.46.29</label> nātyarthavātalāsteṣām
                        mudgādṛṣṭhi prasādanāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         pradhānā haritās tatra vanyā mudgasamāḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.30"><label>1.46.30</label> vipāke madhurāḥ proktā
                        masūrā vaddha varccasaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         maukuṣthakāḥ krimiharāḥ kalāyāḥ pracūrānilāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.31"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.32"/>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.33"><label>1.46.33</label> hareṇava satīnāś ca
                        vijñeyābhinnavarccasaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         ṛte mudgam asūrābhyām anye cādhmānakārakāḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.34"><label>1.46.34</label> māṣo
                        gururbbhinnapurīṣamūtraḥ snigdho 'tha vṛṣyo madhuro 'nilaghnaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         santarppaṇaḥ stanyakaro viśeṣād valapradaḥ śukrakaphāvahaś ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.35"><label>1.46.35</label> kaṣāyabhāvān na
                        purīṣabhedī na mūtralo naiva lavāsa karttā |
                        <caesura/>
                         svādurvripāke madhuronasāndraḥ santarppaṇastanyarucipradaś ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.36"><label>1.46.36</label> māṣaiḥ samānaṃ phalam
                        ātmaguptam uktañ ca kākāṇḍuphalaṃ tathaiva |
                        <caesura/>
                         āraṇyamāṣā guṇataḥ pradiṣṭā rūkṣāḥ kaṣāyā avidāhinaś ca || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.37"><label>1.46.37</label> uṣṇaḥ kulattho rasataḥ
                        kaṣāyaḥ kaṭūrvvipāke kaphamārutaghnaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śikrāśmarīgulmanisūdanaś ca sāṅgrāhikaḥ pīnasakāsahantā || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.38"><label>1.46.38</label> ānāhamedo
                        gudakīlahikkāśvāsāpahaḥ śoṇitapittakṛc ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         valāsa hantā nayanāmayaghno viśeṣato vanyakulattha uktaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.39"><label>1.46.39</label> īṣatkaṣāyo madhuraḥ
                        satiktaḥ sāṃgrāhikaḥ pittakarās tathoṣṇaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tilo vipake kaṭūko valiṣṭhaḥ snigdho vraṇo lepana pathyād uktaḥ
                        || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.40"><label>1.46.40</label> dantyo 'gnimedhājanano
                        'lpamūtraḥ svaryo 'tha keśyo 'nilahā guruś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         tileṣu sarvvaṣ eva sitaḥ pradhāno madhyaḥ sito hīnatarās tathānye
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.41"><label>1.46.41</label> yavaxkaṣāyo madhuro
                        himaś ca kaṭur vvipāke kaphapittahantā |
                        <caesura/>
                         vraṇeṣu pathyāstilavac ca nityaṃ pravṛddhamūtro vahuvātavarccāḥ
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.42"><label>1.46.42</label>
                        sthairyāgnimedhāsvaravarṇṇakṛc ca sapicchilaḥ sthūlavilekhanaś ca
                        |
                        <caesura/>
                         medo 'nilastṛtṛraṇo 'tha rūkṣaḥ prasādanaḥ śoṇitapittayoś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.43"><label>1.46.43</label> ebhir gguṇair hīnataraiś
                        ca kiñcid vidyād yavebhyo 'pi yavān aśeṣān |
                        <caesura/>
                         godhūma ukto madhuro guruś ca valyaḥ sthiraḥ śukravalapradaś ca
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.44"><label>1.46.44</label> snigdho 'tha śīto
                        'nilapittahantā sandhānakṛc chleṣmakaraḥ saraś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         rūkṣaḥ kaṣāyo viṣaśokhaśukravalāsadṛṣṭikṣayakṛdvidāhī || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.45"><label>1.46.45</label> kaṭurvvipāke madhuraś ca
                        simvaḥ prabhinnaviṇmārutapittalaś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         śitāśitā pītakinaḥ kuvarṇṇā bhavanti ye 'nyekisarāś ca simvāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.46"><label>1.46.46</label> yathoditas te guṇataḥ
                        pradhānā jñeyās tathārddrā rasapākayoś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         sahādvayaṃ mūlakapādikā ca kusiddhavallīprabhavāś ca śimbāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.47"><label>1.46.47</label> jñeyā vipāke madhurā
                        rase ca valapradāḥ pittanibarhaṇāś ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidāhavantaś ca bhṛśañ ca rūkṣā viṣṭabhya jīryanty anilapradāś ca
                        || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.48"><label>1.46.48</label> rucipradāś caiva
                        sudurjjarāś ca sarvvāḥ smṛtā vaidalikāś ca śimbāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṭur vvipāke madhurānilaghno vidāhibhāvādahitaḥ kusumbaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.49"><label>1.46.49</label> uṣṇātasī
                        svādurasānilaghnī pittolvaṇā syāt kaṭukā vipāke |
                        <caesura/>
                         pāke rase cāpi kaṭupradiṣṭa ssiddhārthakaḥ śoṇitapittakopī || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.49ef"><label>1.46.49ef</label> snigdhoṣṇatiktaḥ
                        kaphavātahantā tathā guṇaś cāśitasarṣapo pi || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.50"><label>1.46.50</label> anārttavaṃ vyādhihatam
                        aparyāgatam eva ca |
                        <caesura/>
                         abhūmijan navamvāpi na dhānyaṅ guṇavat smṛtaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.51"><label>1.46.51</label> navan dhānyam abhiṣyandi
                        laghu samvat saroṣitaṃ |
                        <caesura/>
                         vidāhi guru viṣṭambhi virūḍham vātakopanaṃ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.52ab"><label>1.46.52ab</label> śālyādeḥ
                        sarṣapāntasya dvividhasyāsya bhāgaśaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kālapramāṇasaṃskāro mātrā cāsmin parīkṣyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.53"><label>1.46.53</label> ata ūrddhvam
                        māṃsavarggam upadekṣyāmaḥ || tatra jaleśayā anūpā grāmyāḥ |
                        kravyabhuja | ekasaphajāṅgalāś ceti | ṣaṇmāṃsavarggā bhavanti |
                        teṣām uttarottarāḥ pradhānatamās te punar dvividhā ānūpajāṅgalāś
                        ca | tatra jāṅgalavarggo 'ṣṭavidhaḥ | tatra jaṃghālā viṣkirāḥ
                        pranudā guheśayāḥ prasahāḥ parṇṇamṛgāḥ | vileśayā grāmyāś ceti ||
                        teṣañ jaṅghālaviṣkirau pradhānatamau | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.54"><label>1.46.54</label> tatra jaṅghalā
                        eṇahariṇarkuraṅga ṛṣya
                        rālakṛtamālaśalabhaśvadaṃṣṭrīcāruṣkavṛṣatemṛgamātṛkāprabhṛtayaḥ
                        kaṣāya madhurā laghavo vātapittaharāstīkṣṇā vastiviśodhanāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.55"><label>1.46.55</label> kaṣāyamadhurā hṛdyaḥ
                        pittāsṛkkapharogahā |
                        <caesura/>
                         sāṅgrāhī rocano valyas teṣām eṇo jvarāpahaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.56"><label>1.46.56</label> madhuro madhuraḥ pāke
                        doṣaghno laghudīpanaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śītalo vaddhaviṭmūtraḥ sugandhir hariṇaḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.59"><label>1.46.59</label>
                        lāvatittirikapiñjalavarttīrakavarttakavātīkācakorakala-viṅkamayūrakrakaropacakrakakukkuṭā
                        viṣkirā laghavaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.60ab"><label>1.46.60ab</label> śītalāmadhurāḥ
                        kaṣāyā doṣaśamanāś ca || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.60cd"><label>1.46.60cd</label> sāṃgrāhī dīpanaḥ
                        śītaḥ kaṣāyamadhuras tathā | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.60ef"><label>1.46.60ef</label> lāvaḥ kaṭuvipākaś
                        ca- sannipāteṣu pūjitaḥ || </l>


                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.61"><label>1.46.61</label> īṣadgurūṣṇamadhuro vṛṣyo
                        medhāgnivarddhanaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         tittiriḥ sarvvadoṣaghno grāhī varṇṇaprasādanaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.62"><label>1.46.62</label> raktapittaharaḥ śīto
                        laghuś cāpi kapiñjalaḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         kaphottheṣu ca rogeṣu mandavāte ca śasyate || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.63"><label>1.46.63</label> vātapittaharā vṛṣyā
                        medhāgnibalavarddhanāḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.64"><label>1.46.64</label> laghavaḥ krakarā hṛdyās
                        tathāś caivopacakrakāḥ ||
                        <caesura/>
                         kaṣāyaḥ svādulavaṇaḥ svaryaḥ keśyo rucipradaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.65"><label>1.46.65</label> mayūraḥ svaramedhāgnir
                        ddṛkchrotrendriyadārḍhyakṛt ||
                        <caesura/>
                         snigdhoṣṇo 'nilahā vṛṣyaḥ svedaḥ svarabalāvahaḥ | </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.146.66"><label>146.66</label> bṛṃhaṇaḥ kukkuṭo vanyas
                        tadvad grāmyo gurus tu saḥ ||</l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.67"><label>1.46.67</label>
                        kapotapārāvatabhṛṅgarājaparabhṛtayaṣṭīmakakuliṅgagokṣvelakaḍiṇḍimāṇaśatapatramātṛliṅgabhedāśiśukasārikāvaggulīlaṭvāladūṣakasūgṛhākhañjarīṭakadātyūhaprabhṛtayaḥ
                        pranudāḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.68"><label>1.46.68</label> kaṣāyamadhurā rūkṣāḥ
                        phalāhārānilāvahāḥ |
                        <caesura/>
                         śleṣmapittaharāḥ śītā baddhamūtrālpavarccasaḥ || </l>

                    <l xml:id="SS.1.46.69"><label>1.46.69</label> sarvvadoṣakaras teṣām
                        bhedāsī maladūṣaṇaḥ |
